country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.10
	title = ww1_italy.10.t
	desc = ww1_italy.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	fire_only_once = no
	trigger = {
		date > 1911.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ITA_you_can_stop_now
		}
		tag = ITA
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.10.a
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_political_power = -10
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_political_power_var = -0.01
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_war_pp_loss = 0.01
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_war_pp_display = 1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_we_want_a_war
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.002
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.002
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.12
	title = ww1_italy.12.t
	desc = ww1_italy.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_luigi_luzzatti
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Accept Ultimatum
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.12.a
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.38
				days = 1
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 448
						state = 450
						state = 1060
						state = 1061
						state = 661
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = ITA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 663
						state = 273
						state = 1122
						state = 1124
						state = 1128
						state = 1128
						state = 567
						state = 754
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = LBA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				TUR = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = ITA
						ratio < 0.6
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Reject Ultimatum
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.12.b
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.37
				days = 1
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = blank
		effect_tooltip = {
			ITA = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = TUR
					type = take_claimed_state
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Offer Italy protectorates
		name = ww1_italy.12.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_ROM.tt
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.25
				days = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = effects_if_accept_ITA
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 448
						state = 1060
						state = 661
						state = 273
						state = 567
						state = 1061
						state = 450
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = CYR
			}
			CYR = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TUR
					relation = military_access
					active = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = empty_focus
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CYR_vittorio_emanuele_iii
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = colonial_government
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = ww1_italy.25.b
		ITA_house_of_cards_update = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_right_swing_support = 3
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_right_swing_support_3
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_socialist_pm_support = -3
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_socialist_support_3_mius
		TUR = {
			country_event = ww1_italy.26
		}
		set_global_flag = italo_turkish_war
		ITA = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TUR
				type = take_claimed_state
			}
		}
		news_event = ww1_italianturkish.8
		hidden_effect = {
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.32
	title = ww1_italy.32.t
	desc = ww1_italy.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_democratic_parlament
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.32.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						ITA_maximalist_power = ITA_reformist_socialist_power
					}
					check_variable = {
						ITA_maximalist_power > ITA_reformist_socialist_power
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_italy.52
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					ITA_maximalist_power < ITA_reformist_socialist_power
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_italy.53
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.61
	title = ww1_italy.61.t
	desc = ww1_italy.61.d
	picture = GFX_french_parliament
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.61.a
		clr_country_flag = ITA_vote_of_no_confidence_flag
		complete_national_focus = ITA_fall_of_the_great
		#Salandra Conservative Tree
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = ITA_libya_lose
				}
				check_variable = {
					ITA_left_wing_focuses_taken > -1
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.69
				days = 2
			}
		}
		#Radical Tree
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_the_conductor_and_his_choir
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = ITA_libya_lose
					has_completed_focus = ITA_church_as_tool_of_the_state
					check_variable = {
						ITA_right_wing_focuses_taken > -1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.298
				days = 2
			}
		}
		#Socialist Tree
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = ITA_libya_lose
					has_global_flag = ITA_not_done_libya_war
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.93
				days = 2
			}
		}
		#Luigi wahoo
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = ITA_libya_lose
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union
							has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union
						}
					}
				}
				has_completed_focus = ITA_male_suffrage
				has_completed_focus = ITA_sway_economic_experts
				has_completed_focus = ITA_shore_up_the_classic_liberals
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.297
				days = 2
			}
		}
		#Pollio dictatorship
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = ITA_male_suffrage
					has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union
					has_completed_focus = ITA_the_conductor_and_his_choir
					has_global_flag = ITA_libya_lose
					has_global_flag = pollio_dies
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.318
				days = 2
			}
		}
		#soninno 
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = ITA_libya_lose
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union
							has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = ITA_male_suffrage
						has_completed_focus = ITA_sway_economic_experts
						has_completed_focus = ITA_shore_up_the_classic_liberals
					}
				}
			
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.335
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ww1_italy.96
	title = ww1_italy.96.t
	desc = ww1_italy.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = ITA_treaty_of_ouchy
		clr_global_flag = ITA_not_done_libya_war
		set_global_flag = libyan_crisis_resolved
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = TUR
			white_peace = LBA
			ITA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_libya.6
					days = 5
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR
					has_state_flag = fallen_to_italy_ITA_TUR_war
				}
				transfer_state_to = ITA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 450
						state = 448
						state = 1061
						state = 1060
						state = 663
						state = 1157
						state = 1156
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = ITA
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = ITA_give_rhodes
				}
				899 = {
					transfer_state_to = ITA
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 1121
						state = 450
						state = 273
						state = 1122
						state = 1124
						state = 1128
						state = 1123
						state = 567
						state = 661
						state = 754
						state = 1155
						state = 1154
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = LBA
			}
			LBA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ITA
					modifier = large_decrease
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.96.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			LBA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ITA
					modifier = large_decrease
				}
			}
			white_peace = TUR
			white_peace = LBA
			ITA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_libya.6
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Socialists blow up rail 
country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.208
	title = ww1_italy.208.t
	desc = ww1_italy.208.d
	picture = GFX_french_parliament
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		has_war_with = TUR
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = libyan_crisis_resolved
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 75
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.208.a
		set_global_flag = ITA_broken_railroads
		unlock_decision_tooltip = ITA_fix_railroads
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ITA
				is_core_of = ITA
				OR = {
					state = 117
					state = 156
					state = 115
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = ITA_broken_railroads_idea
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
	}
}

add_namespace = ww1_italy_dev
# ITALIAN DEVELOPER Events
country_event = {
	# Reset navy variables 1910
	id = ww1_italy_dev.1
	title = ww1_italy_dev.1.t
	desc = blank
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy_dev.1.a
		set_variable = {
			ITA_industrial_capacity_dockyard = -0.25
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_speed = -0.5
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_naval_defense_factor = -0.45
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_org = -0.45
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_see_subs = -0.15
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_oopsies = 0.25
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_exp = -0.45
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_weather = 0.4
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_metal_shark_bite = -0.1
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_visible_on_surface = 0.05
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy_dev.2
	title = ww1_italy_dev.2.t
	desc = blank
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy_dev.2.a
		set_variable = {
			ITA_war_strikes_var = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_strikes_mission_timeout = 60
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy_dev.2.b
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_war_strikes_var = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy_dev.2.c
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_war_strikes_var = -1
		}
	}
}
